 a fresh report by the Economic Advisor to the Finance Ministry has suggested a minimum rate of 12 per cent for GST, a moderate rate of 17 to 19 per cent for services and products and a top rate of 40 per cent
 in teenon daron kii gaharaai main janaa jaruri he
 The minimum rate of 12 per cent means that now the unit rates will be over in the center and state regarding excise and VAT, ie all the products which are under 6-8 per cent tax will be taxed at 12 per cent
 duusari dar ke tahat sarvice tex 14
 Will rise from 5% to 19%
 ho saktaa he petro utpaadon ke liye ek nai dar aae jo 20 fisadi ke irdagird hogi
 a 40 per cent rate is proposed for luxury products
 agar daren itani bhi rahen to bhi jiesti hamen bahut mahangaa padegaa
 The GST structure of "higher consumption and lower tax on earnings" derives from the old principle that we needed to change
 kai bade sudhaaron ke baavjood ham apane kar dhaanche ko aadhunik, sahaj or utsaahi nahin bana sake
 In the countries of the world, there is more tax on earnings and limited tax on consumption, but India's finance ministers gain popularity by reducing tax and corporate tax, while excise, service tax etc
 prove themselves smart by increasing the indirect rate
 direct tex kaa phayda ek chote-se varg ko miltaa he lekin indirect tex badhate hi bahut badi aabaadi kii khapat simit ho jaati he
 The basic principle of tax says that the tax base should decrease with increasing tax base
 lekin arthvyavastha main growth ke saath utpaadan, khapat or karadaataaon kii taadaad badaae ke baavjood indirect tex (exise, sarvice tex, ses, sarcharge) lagaataar bade hai
 In spite of lowering of income tax and corporate tax rates, the number of taxpayers has barely reached four crore people, which is only three per cent of the population
 waite ko lekar hamaara tajurba taakid karata he ki jiesti kii adhiktam dar tay karne kaa suzav upyogi he
 In 2005, Value Added Tax was introduced in the state instead of Sales Tax
 usamen bhi teen tarah kii daren prastaavit thim lekin lagu hone ke teen saal ke bheetar hi puraa anushaasan hawa ho gaya
 Now different states have different taxes on the same product and most of the products have gone into the slab of higher tax rates after VAT is implemented
 oonchi kar daren kaarobaar ko mushkil banane kii sabase badi vajah hai isliye kaarobaari sahajata kii bahasein bhi kar dhaanche par aakar thahar jaati hai

 is prakriya main desh main utpaadan mahangaa hua or nivesh kam or udyogon kii pratispardhaatmakataa ghatati gai
 Targets to increase competition and demand can be achieved only by keeping GST rates down
 bharat main karon kii peedi badalane kaa vakt aa rahaa he

 inamen kanjeshan tex, polution tex, green energy tex honge jo duniya ke deshon main aajamaae ja rahe hai
 Prior to the introduction of these new taxes, it is necessary to reduce the indirect tax, which would cost the general economic consumption, otherwise India's tax structure will be badly inconsistent and will destroy the expectations of entrepreneurship, demand and investment
 darasal tex kii bahes sarkari kharch kam karne kii taraf mudgai chahie
 Due to populist spending, the tax on consumption (indirect) has been squeezed
 sarkaron ko apana aakaar or bhoomika simit kerani hogi taaki khapat sicodere vaali tex thopane kii aadat se nijaat mil sake
 It is not necessary that GST be passed in this session of Parliament, it is more important that we get such GST which reduces our troubles as consumers and investors
 agar oonche tex vaala jiesti lagu hua to iske nattejey na keval aarthik taur par visphotak honge balki raajnneetik taur par bhi inkaa vipareet asar hoga
 In the latest discussion of GST, it is very important to encounter these questions, whether the current structure of GST will ease investment and business in India? Will GST remove the inconsistencies in the tax structure that has led us to become a country of heavy taxes on consumption, which strangles demand and expectations of better living standards? And will we be able to see a system in place after GST that inspires the government not to impose taxes but to limit wasteful spending? These three questions are related to each other and consumers, traders and investors need appropriate answers to these questions from the debate of Parliament because a single poor GST will leave us nowhere

 Today is the birthday of Konkona Sen Sharma, one of the best actress of Indian cinema
 konkana ne bachapan se hi acting shuru kar di thi or aaj bhi ek se badhkar filmon kaa hissaa banati rahati hai
 Let's know some special things about Konkona
 1
 Konkana was born on 3 December 1979 in Kolkata
 2
 Konkanke's father is a famous journalist and science writer Mukul Sharma and mother film director and actor Aparna Sen
 mata pita donon ke sarnem ko konkana apane naam ke aage lagaati hai
 3
 konkana ne kolkatake kalakatta international skool or saint stephen college se padhai kii he
 4
 konkana ne 1983 kii bengali film indira se child artist ke rup main filmon main kaam shuru kiya
 5
 bade hone parkonkana ne bengali film 'ek je aache kanya'se filmon main entry maari
 Konkona had a negative character in the film
 6
 In 2002, Konkona starred in the famous filmmaker Rituparno Ghosh's film Titli, which also featured Konkana's mother Aparna Sen and Mithun Chakraborty
 7
 Konkona directed the English-language film 'mr
 and Mrs
 Iyer 'and Konkona also received the National Award for Best Actress of the year for that film
 8
 In 2005, Konkona played the role of a journalist in Madhur Bhandarkarki's film 'page 3' and the film was also awarded the National Award
 9
 Konkana also played an important role in Vishal Bharadwaj's 'omkara' film for which she received the National Award for Best Supporting Actress
 10
 After a love affair of 3 years, Badakonkana married actor Ranveer Shorey and they both have a beta 'harun'
 kuch vakt pehle ranvir or konkana ne aapasi baatcheet ke baad ek duusare se alag hone kaa bhi faisla kar liya he or donon abhi saath nahin hai

 3 agast 1916 ko badaayun main janmen shakeel ke pita mohammad jamaal ahamed kadri chaahate the ki unka betaa behatar taiyaar ho

 Shakeel's specialty is also seen in the writing of film songs

 Iniesta gave a great pass from the right end to Cesc Fabregas, who gave a cross to Silva while speeding and he had no problem getting it inside the goal from the header
 italy ko dhimi shuruyaat kaa khamiyaja bhugatna padaa
 The team was forced to make changes early on when Giorgio Chilleni was injured and the coach replaced Balzareti in the left back
 italy ko bhi iske baad mauka mila lekin antonio casaano spain ke golkeeper iker kasilas ko chakaane main naakaam rahe or unka dhimaa shot thaamne main golkeeper ko koi dikkat nahin hui
 Italian striker Casano got a chance again, but this time Real Madrid goalkeeper Cassilas shot his way out of the box with his scathing shot
 spain ne madhyantar se thik pehle apane hamalon main teji dikhaai jiskaa use phayda bhi mila jab puure toornament main shandaar pradarshan karne vaale jordi alba ne 41wein minute main jaavi ke shandaar paas par gend ko gol kii raah dikhaa di
 Prandelli replaced Antonio Di Natale at the time of Kasano's replacement
 di natale ne maidan par utarate hi apni upasthiti darj karai
 His header on Ebate's cross went over the goal while minutes later he again managed to penetrate the Spanish defense but this time his attempt was thwarted by Casillas
 duusari taraf buphone ne febregas ke prayaas ko naakaam kiya
 The Italian team was lucky during this time, despite Sergio Ramos's header being placed in the hand of Leonadre Benucci, the referee did not see it and did not give a penalty kick
 tippaniyan Expecting a return to Italy ended when Mota had to be taken out on a stretcher due to a hamstring strain, about half an hour before the match was over and Prandelli's team had to play the rest of the match with 10 players
 vah isse paanch minute pehle hi ricoderen motolivo kii jagah maidan par utre the
 After this there was a slight lack of thrill but Torres changed the atmosphere to get on the field
 unhone jaavi ke paas par 84wein minute main team kii ore se teesraa gol daaga jabaki iske baad chelsi ke apane saathi khilaadi mata ko 88wein minute main chauthaa gol karne main madad kii
 Andrés Iniesta and Javi played a key role in Spain's victory, scoring goals from David Silva (14th minute), Jordi Alba (41st minute) and Fernando Torres (84th minute)
 juaan marta (88wein minute) ne team kii ore se chauthaa gol daaga
 Torres, who scored a decisive goal against Germany in Euro 2008, also became the first player to score a goal in the finals of two European Championships during this time
 euro toornament ke itihaas main khitaabi jeet ke dauraan yah jeet kaa sabase bada antar he
 Earlier in 1972, West Germany defeated the Soviet Union 3–0
 spain iske saath hi germany (1972, 1980 or 1992) ke alaava teen baar euro khitaab jeetne vaali ekmaatr team banane kii uplabdhi bhi hasil kii
 Spain had previously won titles in 1964 and 2008
 duusari taraf nokout main germany or england jaisi tiimon ko baahar kaa rasta dikhaane vaali ajoori team aaj bilkul bhi lay main nahin dikhi
 Mario Balotelli, the hero of the semi-final win against Germany, did not get any benefit from his efforts while Andrea Pillere was held up by the Spanish midfield
 italy ko iske alaava apane sabhi sthanapann khilaadiyon ko istemaal karne ke kaaran antim 30 minute main sirf 10 khilaadiyon ke saath khelnaa padaa jisase spain kii raah or bhi aasaan ho gai or usne is dauraan do or gol daage
 Thiago Mota was injured in the 61st minute shortly after landing as Italy's third and final substitute player, forcing the team to play with 10 players the rest of the time
 antarrashtriya str par pichley kuch samay main spain ke dabadabe kaa andaja is baat se lagaaya ja saktaa he ki pichley 51 pratispardhi maichon main use sirf do baar haar kaa munh dekhnaa padaa he
 This is the first time since Antwerp Olympic 1920 when Spain defeated Italy in competitive football within 90 minutes
 italy ke coach sejaar prendeli ke liye haalanki yah muqabla niraashajanak rahaa
 Under his guidance, Italy had not lost any of the 15 matches earlier and the team did not score a single goal in 10 matches during this time but today their players did not play in front of Spain's offensive game
 spain ne match main tufaani shuruyaat kii
 Out of the semi-finals against Portugal, Cesc Fabregas returned to Spain's starting line-up and played in his 'false Nine' role during a 1–1 draw in a Group c match against Italy on 10 June 
 italy ke coach prendeli ne bhi apane shuruaati line ap main ek badaalav karte hue federico balajareti kii jagah ignajiyo ebet ko utaaya

 This is the largest margin of victory during title wins in Euro tournament history
 isse pehle pashchim germany ne 1972 main soviet sangh ko 3-0 se haraaya tha
 Spain also achieved the feat of becoming the only team to win the Euro title three times apart from Germany (1972, 1980 and 1992)
 spain ne isse pehle 1964 or 2008 main khitaab jeeta tha
 On the other hand, the Ajuri team, which showed the way out to teams like Germany and England in the knockout, did not appear in any rhythm today
 germany ke khilaaf semifinal jeet ke hero mario baloteli ko apane prayaason kaa koi laabh nahin mila jabaki andria pilre ko spain ke midfield ne ulajhaa kar rakhaa
 Italy also had to play with just 10 players in the final 30 minutes due to using all their substitute players, making Spain's path even easier and scoring two more goals in the meantime
 thiyago motaa italy ke tisare or antim sthanapann khilaadi ke rup main utarane ke kuch der baad hi 61wein minute main chotil ho gaye the jisase team ko baaki samay 10 khilaadiyon ke saath khelnaa padaa
 At the international level, Spain's dominance in the recent past can be gauged from the fact that it has suffered only two defeats in the last 51 competitive matches
 entwarp olympic 1920 ke baad yah pehla mauka he jab spain ne pratispardhi footbal main 90 minute ke bheetar italy ko haraaya he
 However, the match was disappointing for Italy coach Sezar Prandelli
 italy ne unke maargdarshan main isse pehle 15 maichon main se ek bhi nahin ganvaaya tha or team ne is dauraan 10 maichon main ek bhi gol nahin khaaya lekin aaj spain ke aakraamak khel ke saamne unke khilaadiyon kii ek nahin chali
 Spain made a stormy start to the match
 portugal ke khilaaf semifinal se baahar sesk febregas kii spain ke shuruyaat line ap main vaapasi hui or vah apni ‘falls nine’ kii bhoomika main hi khele jo unhone italy ke khilaaf 10 june ko group si match main 1-1 ke drow ke dauraan nibhaai thi
 Italian coach Prandelli also made a change in his starting line up, replacing Ignazio Abate in place of Federico Balzareti
 jaavi ko 10wein minute main gol karne kaa shandaar mauka mila lekin unka damdaar shot golkeeper jiyanluigi buphone ke upar se nikal gaya
 However, Spain took the lead after four minutes
 iniesta ne daaen chor se sesk febregas ko shandaar paas diya jinhone teji dikhaate hue silva ko cross diya or unhen ise hader se gol ke andar pahunchane main koi dikkat nahin hui
 Italy suffered the brunt of a slow start
 team ko shuruyaat main hi badlaav karne ko majaboor hona padaa jab jeeorgio chileni chotil ho gaye or coach ne unki jagah left back main balajareti ko utaara
 Italy also got a chance after that but Antonio Casano failed to impress Spain goalkeeper Iker Casillas and the goalkeeper had no problem stopping his slow shot
 italy ke striker casaano ko dobaaraa mauka mila lekin is baar riyal madrid ke golkeeper kasilas ne box ke baahar se maare unke dandanaate hue shot ko baahar kaa rasta dikhaa diya
 Spain accelerated their attacks just before the intermission, which also benefited them when Jordi Alba, who had a great performance throughout the tournament, showed the ball in the 41st minute on Javi's brilliant pass
 prendeli ne madhyantar ke samay casaano kii jagah antonio di natale ko utaara
 De Natale made his presence known as he landed on the field
 ebet ke cross par unka hader gol ke upar se nikal gaya jabaki kuch minute baad vah dobaaraa spain ke dephence ko bhedane main safal rahe lekin is baar kasilas ne unke prayaas ko naakaam kar diya
 Bufon on the other hand thwarted Fabregas' attempt
 is dauraan italy kii team bhaagyashaalee rahi jab sarjeeo ramos kaa hader leyonadere benuchi ke haath main lagane ke baavjood referi ise nahin dekh paae or unhone penlti kik nahin di
 The comments italy kii vaapasi kii ummid us samay samaapt ho gai jab match khatm hone se lagbhag aadha ghanta pehle motaa ko pair kii mansapeshiyon main khinchaav ke kaaran strachar par baahar le janaa padaa or prendeli kii team ko baaki match 10 khilaadiyon ke saath khelnaa padaa
 Five minutes before that, he landed on the field in place of recorders Motolivo

 Police on Saturday seized stolen CCTV footage from ICICI Bank's ATM
 In the Asola area of south Delhi, the miscreant on Saturday night cut an ATM with a gas cutter and took lakhs of rupees from it
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki ghatana ke vakt atm main kareeb 3 lakh 75 hajaar rupee the
 However, according to the landlord, the ATM had Rs 14 lakh in cash at the time of the incident
 disipi atul thakur ne maamle kii pushti karte hue bataaya ki ghatana ke vakt atm booth par koi guard nahin tha
 Police are seizing CCTV footage installed in the ATM booth to check how many people were at the time of the incident and how much cash was there in the machine
 philhal maidangadhi thana police maamle kii jaanch kar rahi he
 The incident occurred at ICICI Bank's ATM in Asola, Chhatarpur in the Maidan Garhi police station area
 yah atm ilaake ke main road par he
 Before committing the crime, the miscreants sprayed black paint on all cameras outside and inside the ATM, then carefully cut the machine with a cutter and took away all the money kept in it
 makaan maalik ke anusaar jis vakt ye chori hui us samay is atm main 14 lakh rupee the jise badi safai se badmaash le ude or is vaardaat kii jaankaree unhen subah mili jab wo neeche aae

 unka kahana he ki itani majboot or behad surakshit atm ko jab badmaash katkar aaraam se paise le ja sakate hai, to wo log bahut kuch kar sakate hai
